            if (!shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            preloadBannerSdk();

            ONE_TRUST_LIBRARIES.forEach((library) => {
                loadScript(library.url, "text/javascript", library.options);
            });

            if (country === "US") {
                loadCCPAAddon();
            }
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithOneTrustEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

<dl><dd><span class="dablink"><i>For the chapter of the same name, see <a href="/wiki/Chapter_611" title="Chapter 611">Chapter 611</a>.</i></span></dd></dl>
<p><b>Hody Jones</b><sup id="cite_ref-romanization_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-romanization-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> is a great white shark <a href="/wiki/Fish-Men" title="Fish-Men">fish-man</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Captain" class="mw-redirect" title="Captain">captain</a> of the <a href="/wiki/New_Fish-Man_Pirates" title="New Fish-Man Pirates">New Fish-Man Pirates</a> before their downfall,<sup id="cite_ref-mentioned_3-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-mentioned-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup> and a former soldier of the <a href="/wiki/Ryugu_Kingdom" title="Ryugu Kingdom">Neptune Army</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Neptune&#39;s_soldier_4-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Neptune&#39;s_soldier-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> 
</p><p>He is an admirer and militant believer of <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a>'s ideals,<sup id="cite_ref-Arlong_9-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Arlong-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> and the main antagonist of the <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island_Arc" title="Fish-Man Island Arc">Fish-Man Island Arc</a>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Appearance">Appearance</span></h2>
<p>Hody is a grey-skinned <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/great_white_shark" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:great white shark">great white shark</a> fish-man. He had a large belly, with a tattoo of the New Fish-Man Pirates design on the right side as well as a long scar on the left, and muscular arms and legs. His facial features include glaring eyes, with long and distinctive eyelashes, a mouth full of sharp, triangular teeth, and a stub nose. He had long black curly hair, with a long tuft hanging on the left part of his face. His left arm is intricately tattooed, with the <a href="/wiki/Arlong_Pirates" title="Arlong Pirates">Arlong Pirates</a>' <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger" title="Jolly Roger">Jolly Roger</a> near the wrist and several circular designs above it ending with two skulls on the upper arm; he also has some spikes protruding from his bare wrist and circling it all, possibly decorative piercings.<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> His brief fight with <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> left him with a new scar that appears to start below his left shoulder and goes down his chest diagonally to the right, similar to the one <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a> gave Zoro.<sup id="cite_ref-new_scar_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-new_scar-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He sported a pink <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/newsboy_cap" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:newsboy cap">newsboy cap</a>, with a little trident represented on the left side, bearing a resemblance to the same weapon he was sometimes seen carrying around, and a massive scarf seemingly made from a dog-like animal around his neck, with the animal’s head hanging on the left side of his chest. Hody was seen wearing a red open shirt with short sleeves, a wide collar and dark-red spots on the lower part, short blue trousers with a similar pattern but with light-blue spots, a pink sash tied around the waist, and sandals.<sup id="cite_ref-introduction_8-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-introduction-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After overdosing himself on <a href="/wiki/Energy_Steroid" title="Energy Steroid">Energy Steroids</a>, Hody underwent a drastic change in appearance: he no longer had a large belly, being far more muscular than before, with his muscles bulging in size with thick veins appearing, particularly on his arms, and his size greatly increased, being in equal in size to <a href="/wiki/Ikaros_Much" title="Ikaros Much">Ikaros Much</a>, the largest of the New Fish-Man Pirates, while sitting down. His dark hair had lightened exponentially. He no longer wore any headgear, and donned a shirt with the colors reversed from the one he originally wore, with the dark background having turned light and the light spots along the bottom having turned dark.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He also carried his trident on his back.
</p><p>As Noah continued to descend on Fish-Man Island and Hody's hatred grew stronger, the sclera turned red and he was seen with an enlarged jaw about the size of Luffy (though in the anime it was because he consumed more Energy Steroids). He also appears to have grown so much muscle mass that his shirt ripped apart as a result. It is later shown after he is defeated that during his last fight with <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a> that he gained enough muscle mass that he is now the size of the royal princes.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> By the time of his defeat and capture, the crew noted that Hody looked like a monster.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After being defeated and imprisoned, another side effect of the Energy Steroid kicked in- the shortening of the user's lifespan relative to the number of steroids consumed. Unfortunately for Hody, his (and his fellow officers') Energy Steroid abuse has resulted in all of them becoming old and frail- and Hody's appearance has changed into that of an old man's, considerably more aged than his subordinates due to taking an especially large quantity of the steroids. His hair remained white, and nearly all the hair on his upper scalp fell out, causing him to become bald, except for the curled hair that hangs below his neck, which remained intact. He grew a mustache, as well as a goatee several inches long, and his skin wrinkled. He also became incredibly skinny, losing all of his muscle and some of his teeth with the remaining teeth now square instead of sharp, and has become hunched over on bent knees now having to walk with a cane.<sup id="cite_ref-c650p15_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c650p15-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a teenager, he had less sharp facial features, shorter hair, and a leaner build. He wore a newsboy cap with the word "CHECK" imprinted on it and a simple scarf paired with an open dark vest decorated by two sword-like motifs on the front.<sup id="cite_ref-c622p7_16-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c622p7-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Hody_Jones_Pirate_Warriors_3.png/revision/latest?cb=20150328222646" class="image"><img alt="Hody Jones Pirate Warriors 3" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="105" height="84" data-image-name="Hody Jones Pirate Warriors 3.png" data-image-key="Hody_Jones_Pirate_Warriors_3.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/ec/Hody_Jones_Pirate_Warriors_3.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/105?cb=20150328222646" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Hody in <i><a href="/wiki/One_Piece:_Pirate_Warriors_3" title="One Piece: Pirate Warriors 3">One Piece: Pirate Warriors 3</a></i>.

</div></span></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other">Other</span></h4>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Hody_Jones_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest?cb=20180905174344" class="image"><img alt="Hody Jones Anime Concept Art" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="67" height="105" data-image-name="Hody Jones Anime Concept Art.png" data-image-key="Hody_Jones_Anime_Concept_Art.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/c/c6/Hody_Jones_Anime_Concept_Art.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/67?cb=20180905174344" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Hody's concept art from the anime.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/95/Hody_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20211104061937" class="image"><img alt="Hody Digitally Colored Manga" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="100" height="105" data-image-name="Hody Digitally Colored Manga.png" data-image-key="Hody_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/95/Hody_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/100?cb=20211104061937" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Hody in the <a href="/wiki/Digitally_Colored_Manga" title="Digitally Colored Manga">Digitally Colored Manga</a>.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 127px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 127px; height: 127px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dd/Log_Noah_Alt.png/revision/latest?cb=20190515103403" class="image"><img alt="Log Noah Alt" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="75" height="105" data-image-name="Log Noah Alt.png" data-image-key="Log_Noah_Alt.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/dd/Log_Noah_Alt.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/75?cb=20190515103403" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Hody Jones' attire with fur coat from <a href="/wiki/Home_Video_Releases" title="Home Video Releases">One Piece Log Collection</a>.
</div></span></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personality">Personality</span></h2>
<p>Hody is a racist, overly hypocritical, prideful, brutal, and vicious natured fish-man who, like many of his kind, hates humans for leaving <a href="/wiki/Fisher_Tiger" title="Fisher Tiger">Fisher Tiger</a> to die when he could have been saved (which was not true, as Tiger refused human blood due to being betrayed). He proves this by attacking humans within his reach. He, like <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a>, believes that fish-men are the supreme race, demonstrating his arrogance by attacking Gyro's crew with his hands cuffed, showing them that they could easily be destroyed even with the handicap. He then deliberately released the crew, injured but alive, setting them as examples, telling them to spread the word of the New Fish-Man Pirates.
</p><p>Despite the fact that they both looked down on humans, his treatment of humans is even more brutal than Arlong's. He considers his human captives to be expendable and sees them as nothing more than pawns whereas Arlong had left humans alone so long as they paid him "tribute" money periodically. Arlong mainly killed humans to make examples of them when they did not pay up and was content with leaving them be, aside from odd acts to make sure the humans knew who was boss, but Hody will go out of his way to attack humans, such as using them as part of his plan that will almost ensure their deaths, and threatening to kill them outright if they refuse, giving them very little chance to live altogether.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Nothing... Heaven has chosen us to hand down judgement to humanity... and given us power!!
</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Hody's answer to Fukaboshi when asked what humans did to him.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
<p class="mw-empty-elt">
</p>
  </cite></td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
Hody basically grew up basking in the hatred of fish-men towards humanity. He and his crew would hate and fear the day when the animosity between humans and fish-men would fade. This leads Hody and his crew to become bloodthirsty radicals who do not care for the peace of <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island" title="Fish-Man Island">Fish-Man Island</a>. Hody himself believes that heaven has selected him and his crew to hand judgement down to humanity, in spite of the fact that humans did utterly nothing against Hody personally.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup> From his point of view, hatred towards humans is his definition of pride. Hody despises anyone who wants peace with humans especially Otohime, claiming that her preaching was aggravating and he did everything in his power to keep her hopes and dreams from becoming real. Hody's belief of fish-men superiority is so fierce, he fanatically believes that heaven itself has granted him power.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Despite Hody seeing Arlong as a role model, there are several factors that greatly distinguish the two, besides the difference in their levels of cruelty. While Arlong was tight with his wallet and could not pay for <a href="/wiki/Hyouzou" title="Hyouzou">Hyouzou</a> for his services as well as failing to get <a href="/wiki/Vander_Decken_IX" title="Vander Decken IX">Vander Decken IX</a> as his subordinate, Hody managed to make accommodations for these two by being more open with financial compensation and was willing to treat powerful allies as equals instead of being a dominating leader. While Arlong valued and considered his crew as his brothers and was extremely angry when one of his crewmen was used as a shield by Luffy, Hody, on the other hand, does not hold camaraderie in any regard even though he has been close to his officers since they were kids. In fact, Hody had no problem using one of his own subordinates as a shield to protect himself and also taunted Neptune for using himself as a shield to protect his own soldiers from harm, deeming him unworthy to be king because of that. Furthermore, according to <a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a>, while Arlong would not harm his fellow fish-men, Hody will kill any fish-man who has shown sympathy towards humans,<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> even referring to the people who gave their signatures to support the migration as a list of traitors. Also unlike the Arlong Pirates, who demonstrate their pride as Fish-Men by utilizing on their natural strength, Hody and his crew did not care what methods they use to show off their superiority, which was best shown by their heavy abuse of Energy Steroids (as Hody calls Arlong's methods to be barbaric, which the New Fish-Man Pirates believed to a mistake to be learned from). He has gotten so arrogant that he now does not seem to care about anyone but himself and his goal, to the point he is willing to sacrifice 100,000 of his own subordinates without a second thought.
</p><p>Hody is also completely fearless (if not insane and delusional), using <a href="/wiki/Energy_Steroid" title="Energy Steroid">Energy Steroids</a>, a potent drug that increases his strength, knowing the effect also shortens his life (though he apparently did not realize it greatly accelerates one's age instead of simply reducing the lifespan). He appears to have developed an addiction to the drug as he continuously ate it throughout the day and even swallowed a giant handful of steroids at once, whether as to gain an upper hand against his enemies or as painkillers. He also threatened his crewmates for preventing him from overdosing, and his violent nature may have been intensified from the side-effects of the Energy Steroids. This arrogant stubbornness led him to overdose heavily and, in turn, destroyed his body, which even then, did not deter him from hating humanity irrationally. His arrogance also made him extremely shortsighted, as he did not even consider the consequences of allowing the Candy Factory to be destroyed, thereby angering Big Mom, whose own power and crew vastly outmatched anything Hody or his crew were capable of combating.
</p><p>Hody considers King <a href="/wiki/Neptune" title="Neptune">Neptune</a> to be a coward and shows a desire of taking Fish-Man Island from him. He will do whatever is needed to achieve his goals as he joined Neptune's army solely for sheer military knowledge and experience and has no qualms about betraying his former comrades.<sup id="cite_ref-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Hody's cruelty, recklessness, hatred, superiority complex and biased goals led Neptune to refer him as quite selfish. He claims that he is fully willing to give his own life to destroy humanity.
</p><p>Hody has shown a great deal of cunning as he deceived the citizens of Fish-Man Island into believing a human murdered Queen <a href="/wiki/Otohime" title="Otohime">Otohime</a>, stole the Energy Steroids from the royal palace without Neptune suspecting him, and later allied with Vander Decken IX (even though Hody does not really see him as an equal) so as to carry out his plan on infiltrating the near impenetrable Ryugu Palace and in an effort to kill <a href="/wiki/Shirahoshi" title="Shirahoshi">Shirahoshi</a>. Hody is also extremely arrogant and boastful (to the point of being insane), showing that he not only thinks himself above all humans, but also above all his fellow fish-men, and went as far as to call the Straw Hat Pirates and a former <a href="/wiki/Seven_Warlords_of_the_Sea" title="Seven Warlords of the Sea">Warlord of the Sea</a> weak, despite their fearsome reputations and high bounties. Even after he and his crew were completely defeated by the Straw Hat Pirates, got locked away and lost all his strength due to his Energy Steroids overdose, Hody remains too arrogant to accept his loss. He is also shown to be quite ignorant, as he completely underestimates the power of his enemies as shown when he attempted to fight Luffy, a pirate with a <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>400,000,000 bounty, who completely overpowered him until Hody dragged the battle into the ocean. This ignorance and arrogance extend to the wider world, as he again completely underestimates the World Government and the Emperor's, and those affiliated with them, as his ultimate goal after becoming king was to slay all the other monarchs gathered at the upcoming <a href="/wiki/Levely" title="Levely">Levely</a> to establish fish-man dominance, not even considering the strength of the enemy or the repercussions of such actions.
</p><p>Like many other characters, he has a <a href="/wiki/Laughter_Style" title="Laughter Style">distinctive laugh</a>: "Jahahahaha!"
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationships">Relationships</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Crew">Crew</span></h3>
<p>Hody seems to be someone who would rather handle things himself, evident when he instructed Ikaros Much to stay back after the latter volunteered to go after Crab-Hand Gyro's crew and opted to hunt them down himself.<sup id="cite_ref-deal_it_himself_21-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-deal_it_himself-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He also seems devoted to their cause to the point where he was willing to resort to the use of the Energy Steroids without any fear of the side effects.<sup id="cite_ref-deal_it_himself_21-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-deal_it_himself-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup> Hody has been close to his officers since they were kids. Even though the rest of his crew was shocked at the news that he killed Otohime, the officers themselves already knew. However, Hody does not have any care for his crewmates as shown when he used one of them as a shield. Dosun even admits that Hody will not hesitate to throw his comrades away.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> Hody's utter disregard for loyalty is demonstrated when he attempted to sacrifice all 100,000 comrades simply to kill the Straw Hats and the Fish-Man Island civilians just for the sake of his revenge. His officers, being just as fanatically prejudiced as he is, are willing to die for their cause if Hody insisted.
</p><p>Regardless of that, Hody's subordinates still follow, respect, and support him. They do seem to care about him since they did show concern for him after Zoro had dealt him a grievous wound and when he had an overdose of Energy Steroids. However, when the lower-rank subordinates were begging for mercy from Jinbe after Hody's defeat, they claimed that they followed Hody because they feared him.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Fish-Men">Other Fish-Men</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Arlong">Arlong</span></h4>
<p>Hody deeply respected <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a> and wished to continue his legacy of conquering humans, though he did think Arlong was barbaric and unsophisticated, a mistake that Hody claimed to have learned from and was more prepared as a result.<sup id="cite_ref-Arlong_9-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Arlong-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> He originally planned to become Arlong's right hand man when he became of age and trained hard to achieve that goal.<sup id="cite_ref-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy_10-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> However, after Arlong's defeat, he decided that the <a href="/wiki/Arlong_Pirates" title="Arlong Pirates">Arlong Pirates</a> were nothing more than an empty symbol for human-hating fish-men to gather under, showing no more respect for Arlong as a person, but only caring for his philosophies. He sought to defeat Luffy not for defeating Arlong, but for ending Arlong's ambitions of conquering humans. Nonetheless, Arlong was one of the most influential people in Hody's childhood.<sup id="cite_ref-Hody_takes_Arlong&#39;s_place_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody_takes_Arlong&#39;s_place-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fisher_Tiger">Fisher Tiger</span></h4>
<p>Hody respects <a href="/wiki/Fisher_Tiger" title="Fisher Tiger">Fisher Tiger</a>, the hero of the fish-man race, and despises the humans for refusing to donate blood to Tiger in his greatest hour of need (though in truth Tiger refused the blood transfusion due to it being tainted by humanity's hatred for fish-men, a fact Tiger asked his crew not to reveal). However, upon Jinbe's return to Ryugu Kingdom as a Warlord of the Sea, Hody learned that Tiger wished to be at peace with humans, which did not stand well with Hody's beliefs.<sup id="cite_ref-Tiger&#39;s_ideals_24-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tiger&#39;s_ideals-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> Regardless of this revelation, Tiger's death had made Hody and his officers realize that Tiger was not the "hero" they thought he was.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hatchan">Hatchan</span></h4>
<p>Even as a child, Hody despised <a href="/wiki/Hatchan" title="Hatchan">Hatchan</a> for speaking highly of humans such as <a href="/wiki/Silvers_Rayleigh" title="Silvers Rayleigh">Silvers Rayleigh</a>, and felt the urge to vomit in disgust whenever Hatchan spoke positively about this friendship.<sup id="cite_ref-Hody-Hatchan_26-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody-Hatchan-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Upon Arlong's defeat and Hatchan's return to Fish-Man Island, Hody lost the little (if there was any to begin with) respect he had left for Hatchan for befriending humans.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> Hody refused to listen to Hatchan's opinions <sup id="cite_ref-Arlong_9-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Arlong-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> and had no qualms with allowing Decken to attack him.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Fish-Man_Island_Civilians">Fish-Man Island Civilians</span></h4>
<p>Hody deeply loathes the citizens of Fish-Man Island for not sharing his perspective. Not only did he terrorize the citizens with violence during his uprising, but he also psychologically tormented them by forcing them to step on the fumi-e of their beloved queen. Hody deems them worthless and claims that they are the reason why humans scorn fish-men and also expressed a desire to execute those who gave their signatures for migration, deeming them as traitors and their signatures as a list to track on. During his final battle with Luffy, Hody attempted to kill the citizens by having Noah fall down on Fish-Man Island, wanting them dead rather than seeing them coexist with humans.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Enemies">Enemies</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Humans">Humans</span></h4>
<p>Like the rest of his crew, Hody despises humans, looking down on them with the full intent of conquering them. He believes humans are as worthless as slaves and was willing to use them as disposable pawns for his invasion plan. Despite this, he was willing to grant freedom to those who completed the task he gave them, although the task he gave them had a very low survival chance. He only spared Gyro and his crew so that they could tell the terrors of the fish-man race to the rest of the world. According to <a href="/wiki/Fukaboshi" title="Fukaboshi">Fukaboshi</a>, Hody hates humans more than anyone else, even though he had no reason to other than being raised to hate them emptily.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Monkey_D._Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</span></h4>
<p>Hody has nothing but hatred for <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a> because he destroyed his Idol Arlong's operations in the East Blue and ruining all of his plans. When he heard Luffy had finally made it to Fish-Man Island he was ecstatic for a chance at revenge.  He made the extra effort to kill him during his coup d'état on Ryugu Kingdom, and intended to show Luffy's head as a way to incite fear to the surface world.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup>Even though he was beyond shocked that Luffy defeated half his forces in an instant with a burst of <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, Hody was confident he could end the Straw Hat captain's life and finish what Arlong started. In the end, however, this proved to be his downfall; Luffy showed complete dominance over Hody whether on land or underwater, which caused Hody to recklessly chew down handfuls of Energy Steroids, enhancing his hatred on a slippery slope. Even after suffering a complete defeat and his body broke down to the point of no repair, Hody continuously demanded for Luffy to be brought to him for a rematch.<sup id="cite_ref-c650p15_15-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c650p15-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jinbe">Jinbe</span></h4>
<p>Hody also notes that <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a> and the faction of the Sun Pirates that follow him are an annoyance. Even though Jinbe had no idea that Hody was the one who actually murdered Otohime (until Hody reveals it),<sup id="cite_ref-revelation_of_true_assassin_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-revelation_of_true_assassin-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> he seems to be the only one outside the Fish-Man District to be aware of Hody's dark nature since he had been keeping tabs on Hody while he was plotting something in the Fish-Man District. During the confrontation at Gyoncorde Plaza, Hody stated that he hates Jinbe the most for not being an enemy of humans especially after the death of Fisher Tiger. By cooperating with the very humans who defeated Arlong, the Straw Hat Pirates, Hody considers Jinbe to be lower than Neptune.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>Hody currently has no idea that Jinbe has become a member of the crew he loathes so much.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Otohime">Otohime</span></h4>
<p>Hody despises <a href="/wiki/Otohime" title="Otohime">Otohime</a> for her philosophy of interspecies cooperation between humans, fish-men and merfolks, which clashes against his hatred against humanity. To this end, he personally killed her and destroyed the signatures she worked so hard to gather and then ultimately put her hard work to waste by framing a human for the murder. While celebrating Otohime's death with his comrades, Hody calls it heaven's judgement. During the coup against the Ryugu Kingdom, Hody forced the citizens of Fish-Man Island to step on her portrait, squashing her supporters and insulting her even after her death. He later bragged about killing her in front of everyone and openly ridiculed her ideals. However, even though Otohime died without knowing who shot her, she did not hate her assailant and pleaded for her children to do the same, a wish that Princess Shirahoshi went to great lengths to honor. Hody would go on to further ridicule this mercy and kindness when he was informed about it.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Neptune">Neptune</span></h4>
<p>Hody believes that <a href="/wiki/Neptune" title="Neptune">Neptune</a> is a worthless king because he (from Hody's perspective) lacks pride. He did not enjoy enlisting in the Neptune Army and only sought to gain battle experience for his own self-interest.<sup id="cite_ref-Neptune&#39;s_soldier_4-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Neptune&#39;s_soldier-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> Hody was determined to take King Neptune's reign away from him so he can create a world where humanity is completely enslaved. After Hody successfully captured the king, he attempted to execute him in front of his people. Unfortunately for him, Hody failed due to Luffy's interference. Hody also earned Neptune's hatred when he revealed that he was the one behind his wife's assassination.<sup id="cite_ref-revelation_of_true_assassin_30-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-revelation_of_true_assassin-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> After Hody was defeated, Neptune did not show any rage towards Hody and just had him imprisoned. When Hody became a frail, old man, Neptune expressed his pity towards him.<sup id="cite_ref-c650p16_32-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c650p16-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Vander_Decken_IX">Vander Decken IX</span></h4>
<p>Hody made an alliance with <a href="/wiki/Vander_Decken_IX" title="Vander Decken IX">Vander Decken IX</a>, and stated it was a pleasure to be working together, and that they were equals instead of leader and underling. However, the reason Hody worked with Decken was because he considered Shirahoshi a threat and thought Decken would be the perfect person to kill her, and that he never really saw Decken as an equal, but instead put up with it simply to use him. After he failed to kill the princess, Hody considered Decken useless. When Decken had betrayed him by going against the plan by throwing Noah towards Fish-Man Island, endangering everyone on it including the New Fish-Man Pirates, Hody saw Decken as a traitor. To get revenge and to destroy Fish-Man Island, Hody stabbed Decken so Noah (which was right above Fish-Man Island) would fall down and destroy the island.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Shirahoshi">Shirahoshi</span></h4>
<p>Because of <a href="/wiki/Shirahoshi" title="Shirahoshi">Shirahoshi</a>'s ability to summon Sea Kings, Hody Jones considers her as a threat to his plans.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> Therefore, she is one of the people that he wants to kill the most.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> On the contrary, despite knowing that Hody was the one who killed her mother, Shirahoshi did not bear a grudge against him, nor report his crime to anyone,<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> due to the princess following her mother's final wish of not hating the person who committed the murder. Hody, in return, ridiculed Shirahoshi for her kindness and mercy.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Abilities_and_Powers">Abilities and Powers</span></h2>
<p>As the <a href="/wiki/Captain" class="mw-redirect" title="Captain">captain</a> of the New Fish-Man Pirates, Hody had complete authority over the crew. However, he was stripped of this power when he and his crew were arrested by the Neptune Army.<sup id="cite_ref-c648_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c648-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Usopp noted that Arlong was nothing compared to Hody.<sup id="cite_ref-Water_38-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Water-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> Camie mentioned to Nami that Hody's mind is more dangerous than his strength, with his deep hatred being his drive beyond his physical limits. However, he was shown to be vastly inferior to several of the Straw Hat Pirates, being severely injured by Zoro even while underwater and easily overpowered by Luffy; to compensate, he was forced to gorge on the Energy Steroids to become a match for Luffy. In this overdosed state, Luffy believed Hody's sheer toughness would be enough to earn him a bounty of at least <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>100,000,000,<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> and he critically injured Luffy (piercing through his <a href="/wiki/Haki/Armament_Haki" title="Haki/Armament Haki">Armament Haki</a>) by biting his shoulder.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>   
</p><p>He also has a strong will, as he was largely unaffected by Luffy's <a href="/wiki/Haki/Supreme_King_Haki" title="Haki/Supreme King Haki">Supreme King Haki</a>, although his hand trembled slightly.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Tactical_Skills">Tactical Skills</span></h3>
<p>During his time in the Neptune Army, he was recognized as a particularly talented soldier.<sup id="cite_ref-Neptune&#39;s_soldier_4-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Neptune&#39;s_soldier-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> As such, he gained knowledge and experience of combat techniques on the battlefield. Hody was also shown to be an extensive planner and shrewd captain, carefully managing the core group of the New Fish-Man Pirates so that all its members would share his extremist ideals and intense prejudice towards humanity. He shot Queen Otohime of Fish-Man Island and then framed a nearby human smuggler as his scapegoat, to increase support from the wider island community in persecuting humans. He was also more financially supportive of his members, freely willing to spend money to recruit the services of Hyouzou (something which Arlong was unwilling to do), and was also able to recognize the value of an alliance with Vander Decken IX as an equal partner to kill the potential threat of Princess Shirahoshi.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Physical_Abilities">Physical Abilities</span></h3>
<p>Prior to his body becoming old and frail, as a fish-man, he was ten times stronger than the average human, and twice that in water. As a shark fish-man, his strength was monstrous even by fish-man standards: he was able to completely destroy a massive wall of stone by simply gripping it. After overdosing on Energy Steroids (and before they made him weak), Hody Jones' physical appearance drastically changed, resulting in a more muscular body and bleached-white hair. Also, Hody's strength had increased tremendously. However, after his body became weak and old due to his overdosing, he lost both the boost he got and his natural strength to the point where he needed a stick just to walk, and when he tried to pull apart iron bars, his wrists broke.
</p><p>Like Arlong, Hody is also able to grow his teeth back immediately after they are broken. His removed set of teeth are replaced by a new set in mere moments.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> Also, Hody is capable of entering a kind of berserker mode when he gets angry. His eyes take on an appearance similar to those of <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea Kings</a>. In this state, Hody seems to have gone mad to which Shirahoshi commented that he became far more terrifying than he usually is.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fish-Man_Karate">Fish-Man Karate</span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Karate" title="Fish-Man Karate">Fish-Man Karate</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>Hody was a practitioner of Fish-Man Karate and he showcased it by his manipulation of water. He could hurl simple droplets of water and turn them into deadly bullets with extreme kinetic force.<sup id="cite_ref-Water_38-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Water-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> He could also punch the water to send a shockwave through the water and the victim's body. After overdosing on Energy Steroids, Hody appeared to drip with water even though he was not soaked, suggesting that he had been secreting it. 
</p><p>However, despite his enormous strength, and according to both Luffy and Jinbe, Hody's Fish-Man Karate was at an amateur level. This was shown when he fought Luffy, for while Jinbe could do noticeable damage to the rubber man, Hody's attacks were ineffective. After his body became old and frail as a side-effect of the steroids, he likely lost the ability to perform it altogether.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Weapons">Weapons</span></h3>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6d/Hody_Jone%27s_Trident.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708141353" class="image"><img alt="Hody Jone&#39;s Trident" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="132" data-image-name="Hody Jone&#39;s Trident.png" data-image-key="Hody_Jone%27s_Trident.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/6d/Hody_Jone%27s_Trident.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20230708141353" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Hody's first plainer trident.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Hody%27s_Elaborate_Trident.png/revision/latest?cb=20240307025832" class="image"><img alt="Hody&#39;s Elaborate Trident" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="93" data-image-name="Hody&#39;s Elaborate Trident.png" data-image-key="Hody%27s_Elaborate_Trident.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/18/Hody%27s_Elaborate_Trident.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240307025832" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Hody's more elaborate trident in the manga.
</div></span><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1e/Kirisame_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708141535" class="image"><img alt="Kirisame Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="45" data-image-name="Kirisame Infobox.png" data-image-key="Kirisame_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1e/Kirisame_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20230708141535" class="lazyload" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">Kirisame, Hody's fin blade.
</div></span></div>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Tridents">Tridents</span></h4>
<p>During his raid on the Ryugu Palace, Hody was seen holding a long, thin red <a href="/wiki/Polearm" title="Polearm">trident</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> possibly something he has kept from his old days as a soldier. He managed to defeat Decken with it by stabbing him and then lifting him to block one of Decken's flying axes. In the anime, Hody also threw the trident like a projectile against Zoro.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In the manga, Hody was seen holding a different trident after being struck a grievous wound by Zoro and then revitalizing himself with an Energy Steroid. It was a light-colored one with elaborate design underneath the spikes, similar to the one used by Neptune himself, but much smaller.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, he continued using the plain red one. Later in the manga, he returned to using his original trident.<sup id="cite_ref-Kirisame_Pre-debut_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kirisame_Pre-debut-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Kirisame">Kirisame</span></h4>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Kirisame" title="Kirisame">Kirisame</a></i></dd></dl>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Kirisame" title="Kirisame">Kirisame</a> is a curved blade that Hody puts on his dorsal fin to cut people while swimming at high speed, being sharp enough to slice through a large oarfish and underwater mountains. This further enhances his shark features.<sup id="cite_ref-Kirisame_Pre-debut_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kirisame_Pre-debut-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> The blade was broken by Luffy during their clash in the ocean.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Weapons">Other Weapons</span></h4>
<p>During his assassination of Otohime, he used a rifle to kill her. He showed enough accuracy to shoot her while she was in the middle of a crowd without detection.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup> In the anime, he wielded a long sword in an attempt to execute Neptune.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Energy_Steroids">Energy Steroids</span></h3>
<dl><dd><i>Further information: <a href="/wiki/Energy_Steroid" title="Energy Steroid">Energy Steroid</a></i></dd></dl>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Hody_Attacking_Gyro_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20210531165105" class="image"><img alt="Hody Attacking Gyro Pirates" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="184" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hody Attacking Gyro Pirates.png" data-image-key="Hody_Attacking_Gyro_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Hody_Attacking_Gyro_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210531165105" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Hody_Attacking_Gyro_Pirates.png/revision/latest?cb=20210531165105" class="image"><img alt="Hody Attacking Gyro Pirates" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Hody_Attacking_Gyro_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210531165105" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="184" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hody Attacking Gyro Pirates.png" data-image-key="Hody_Attacking_Gyro_Pirates.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/65/Hody_Attacking_Gyro_Pirates.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20210531165105" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hody_Attacking_Gyro_Pirates.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody attacking the Gyro Pirates while boosted by Energy Steroids.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>By taking the lifespan-reducing <a href="/wiki/Energy_Steroid" title="Energy Steroid">Energy Steroids</a>, which doubled his strength each time he consumed a pill, Hody became far more dangerous than he already was, taking further advantage of his amazing physical strength. The pills were Hody's main source of power for his campaign of terror.
</p><p>Each pill he took doubled his physical strength. During his attack against <a href="/wiki/Gyro" title="Gyro">Crab-Hand Gyro's</a> escaping ship he had taken at least four and while being underwater, granting him strength at least three-hundred-twenty times that of an average human. His jaws were also very powerful as they were all he needed to single-handedly defeat Crab-Hand Gyro, a pirate with a bounty of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>73,000,000, and his <a href="/wiki/Gyro_Pirates" title="Gyro Pirates">entire crew</a>. Swimming with blinding speed, he punched holes in their ship and even ripped the mast off using his jaws.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup> He took multiple gunshots to the back and was completely unharmed.
</p><p>These pills also seemed to regenerate the users' wounds to some extent and take strain off them, as seen when a wounded and seemingly unconscious Hody, given one more pill, managed to stand up in mere seconds and to use his strength to its full extent, stopping the gigantic Neptune with just one hand. This led him to abuse the pills as though they were painkillers.
</p><p>After overdosing on the drug to ease the pain of the scar Zoro gave him, Hody underwent a painful transformation into a much more massive form. In this new form, his strength was greater than ever, allowing him to throw a drop of water with extreme force, sending it a great distance across the island, piercing through people, buildings, coral, and rock alike. Thanks to the Energy Steroids, he was also able to withstand a lot of damage from Luffy in <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques"><b>Gear 2</b></a> and his Armament Haki-enhanced techniques, which destroyed even <a href="/wiki/Pacifista" title="Pacifista">Pacifistas</a>. Also, Hody was able to swim faster than a mermaid as he managed to catch Shirahoshi while she was fleeing.<sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>However, the Energy Steroids came back to do more harm than good as it made his body weak and old after his arrest. When he tried to bust through the prison cell, he screamed in pain as his joints snapped where he tried to draw his strength from.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Past">Past</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Childhood">Childhood</span></h4>
<p>As Hody and his future officers were growing up in the Fish-Man District, they only learned one thing: hate humans. With Arlong as their role-model, they were indoctrinated into believing that fish-men were heaven-sent to rule the world, and they grew to despise humans based on the belief that they are destined to be superior. Hody and his crew looked up to Arlong and his dream.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup> Hody dreamed that one day, he would grow up to be Arlong's right-hand man.<sup id="cite_ref-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy_10-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Sometime later, in the <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_District" title="Fish-Man District">Fish-Man District</a>, a fish-man was preaching in the street about how humans are an inferior species that are running rampant and threatening fish-mankind. Hody Jones listened to this and seemed to take it to heart. Another fish-man was talking about someone who blew up a slave shop on the surface. A memorial wreath was in front of a large picture of the fish-man in question. People were standing around it, saying that he died, but took eight humans with him and caused widespread disaster on the surface. Hody was pleased that humans died while <a href="/wiki/Ikaros_Much" title="Ikaros Much">Ikaros Much</a> was praising the man, saying he wants to be a "hero" too. At another point, Hody and some other children were listening to Hatchan's story about his friendship with a human named Rayleigh. Before Hatchan finished, Hody left in utter disgust.<sup id="cite_ref-Hody-Hatchan_26-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody-Hatchan-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While they were teenagers, Hody and his companions read about Fisher Tiger's exploits at <a href="/wiki/Mary_Geoise" title="Mary Geoise">Mary Geoise</a>. They cheered the <a href="/wiki/Sun_Pirates" title="Sun Pirates">Sun Pirates</a> on thinking that their goal was to destroy humans, not knowing that Fisher Tiger had non-lethal methods.<sup id="cite_ref-c622p7_16-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c622p7-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Neptune_Army_Days">Neptune Army Days</span></h4>
<p>At some point, he joined the Neptune Army only to gain battle experience and not out of loyalty <sup id="cite_ref-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy_10-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> while his future crew became a group of anarchists that attacked fish-men that dealt with blood transfers with humans. During his time as a soldier, he was present in the throne room when <a href="/wiki/Jinbe" title="Jinbe">Jinbe</a>, the captain of the Sun Pirates after Fisher Tiger, spoke with Neptune. Hody seemed displeased upon hearing that Jinbe accepted the position of Warlord of the Sea, and that Tiger actually wanted peace with the humans.<sup id="cite_ref-Tiger&#39;s_ideals_24-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Tiger&#39;s_ideals-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When a <a href="/wiki/World_Noble" title="World Noble">World Noble</a>, Saint <a href="/wiki/Mjosgard" class="mw-redirect" title="Mjosgard">Mjosgard</a>, arrived on the island, Hody was in favor of killing him, considering him to be "the worst trash in the world".<sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> He then looked stunned upon witnessing <a href="/wiki/Shirahoshi" title="Shirahoshi">Shirahoshi</a>'s ability to summon <a href="/wiki/Sea_King" title="Sea King">Sea Kings</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Hody_%26_Assassin.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708141712" class="image"><img alt="Hody &amp; Assassin" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="219" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hody &amp; Assassin.png" data-image-key="Hody_%26_Assassin.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Hody_%26_Assassin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708141712" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Hody_%26_Assassin.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708141712" class="image"><img alt="Hody &amp; Assassin" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Hody_%26_Assassin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708141712" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="219" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hody &amp; Assassin.png" data-image-key="Hody_%26_Assassin.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e7/Hody_%26_Assassin.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708141712" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hody_%26_Assassin.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody framing a human for Otohime's assassination.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>When Otohime was nearly successful in her campaign for peace with humans, Hody paid a human pirate to set fire to the signature box. Amidst the chaos, Hody assassinated Otohime with a rifle. After successfully murdering Otohime, Hody then shot the pirate.<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> When Jinbe and the royal guards found him, Hody deceived them into thinking that the human was the criminal. Jinbe, not suspecting Hody at all, advised him to hide the pirate. Hody ignored Jinbe and declared to everyone that Otohime was assassinated by the human. Every citizen believed Hody as they grieved over Otohime's death and so, Hody successfully demoralized the citizens as well as giving them another reason to hate humans.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Before leaving the Neptune Army, Hody stole <a href="/wiki/Energy_Steroid" title="Energy Steroid">Energy Steroids</a> from the <a href="/wiki/Tamatebako" title="Tamatebako">Tamatebako</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-c650p16_32-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c650p16-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> Back at the Fish-Man District, Hody and his companions celebrated Otohime's death. Hody then presented the Energy Steroids and asked <a href="/wiki/Zeo" title="Zeo">Zeo</a> to mass-produce them.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="After_Arlong.27s_Defeat"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="After_Arlong's_Defeat">After Arlong's Defeat</span></h4>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Arlong_Pirates" title="Arlong Pirates">Arlong Pirates</a> had been defeated by the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, Hody decided to step up to continue where Arlong left off.<sup id="cite_ref-Arlong_9-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Arlong-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy_10-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody_carries_on_Arlong&#39;s_legacy-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He formed the New Fish-Man Pirates and declared the beginning of their quest for vengeance.<sup id="cite_ref-Hody_takes_Arlong&#39;s_place_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hody_takes_Arlong&#39;s_place-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup> At some time, he also captured and enslaved a <a href="/wiki/Surume" title="Surume">Kraken</a> from the North Pole.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Fish-Man_Island_Arc">Fish-Man Island Arc</span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Alliance">The Alliance</span></h4>
<p>Learning from the Arlong Pirates' mistakes, Hody and his crew made thorough preparations to carry on Arlong's will.<sup id="cite_ref-Arlong_9-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Arlong-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> While preparing for his plan to take <a href="/wiki/Fish-Man_Island" title="Fish-Man Island">Fish-Man Island</a>, Hody even manage to recruit <a href="/wiki/Hyouzou" title="Hyouzou">Hyouzou</a> something Arlong himself failed to do because Hody was willing to pay the high price for his services. had his henchmen intercept human pirate crews coming to Fish-Man Island and force them to join the New Fish-Man Pirates, making their experience on Fish-Man Island miserable. Occasionally, some of the human captives attempted to flee only to be made examples by Hody.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When <a href="/wiki/Hammond" title="Hammond">Hammond</a> reported that the Straw Hat Pirates had arrived on Fish-Man Island, Hody expressed his desire to see the captain, <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Monkey D. Luffy</a>, and ordered Hammond to bring Luffy to him.<sup id="cite_ref-debut_2-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-debut-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>When he learned that <a href="/wiki/Gyro" title="Gyro">Gyro</a>'s pirate crew (a pirate crew that swore loyalty to the New Fish-Man Pirates upon entering Fish-Man Island) was fleeing Fish-Man Island to escape the clutches of the New Fish-Man Pirates, Hody decided to deal with them himself. He took some Energy Steroids and confronted the pirates after putting his hands in handcuffs. With his jaws alone, he gave the pirates a complete and utter defeat. Hody decided to spare their lives in order to allow them to float to the surface, so that they can spread word of the terror of the New Fish-Man Pirates. He then declared that the New Fish-Man Pirates will overthrow King <a href="/wiki/Neptune" title="Neptune">Neptune</a>, take Fish-Man Island by force, and show the world that fish-men are the supreme race.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Pirate_Alliance_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230118175734" class="image"><img alt="Pirate Alliance Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Pirate Alliance Infobox.png" data-image-key="Pirate_Alliance_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Pirate_Alliance_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230118175734" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Pirate_Alliance_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20230118175734" class="image"><img alt="Pirate Alliance Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Pirate_Alliance_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230118175734" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Pirate Alliance Infobox.png" data-image-key="Pirate_Alliance_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/15/Pirate_Alliance_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230118175734" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Pirate_Alliance_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody's alliance with Vander Decken IX.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Later in <a href="/wiki/Noah" title="Noah">Noah</a>, he was joined by <a href="/wiki/Vander_Decken_IX" title="Vander Decken IX">Vander Decken IX</a>. After Decken put on a glove, they shook hands, forming an alliance. They agreed to take down Neptune, crush the Neptune Army, and cause the <a href="/wiki/Ryugu_Kingdom" title="Ryugu Kingdom">kingdom</a> to crumble.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As they set their plan into motion, Hatchan appeared and tried to talk the New Fish-Man Pirates out of going through with the operation. Hody expressed his disappointment towards Hatchan, saying that he has gotten soft and allowed him to become a target of Vander Decken IX. Once Hatchan had been dealt with, Hody then told a group of captive pirates about how they will take part in the operation. He explained to them that Decken will throw them at Hard-Shell Tower in the Ryugu Palace. Once they are inside, they will open the connection corridor to the palace which will allow the New Fish-Man Pirates to invade. Hody went on saying that he was not concerned about whether they live or die and that they were nothing more than pawns for them to use.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="The_Coup_d.27.C3.89tat"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Coup_d'État">The Coup d'État</span></h4>
<p>Hody was then seen heading to the Ryugu Palace while riding on top of the sea monsters with his crew and Decken. Once they entered the palace, they met the Straw Hats and the already subdued and tied-up King Neptune and the Ryugu Palace guards. Hody commented that this seemed way too convenient.
