King Neptune quickly accused Decken of kidnapping Shirahoshi which made Decken realize that the Mermaid Princess was no longer in the palace. Hody calmed down Decken saying that he could find her location using <a href="/wiki/Mato_Mato_no_Mi" title="Mato Mato no Mi">his ability</a>. Decken went after Shirahoshi leaving Hody to take care of things in the palace.
</p><p>After seeing that Hody has an Arlong tattoo, <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> went to an unknown location. When the <a href="/wiki/Minister_of_the_Right" title="Minister of the Right">Minister of the Right</a> cursed Hody, a former soldier of the Neptune Army, for causing chaos on Fish-Man Island, Hody revealed that he only joined the army to gain experience. Hody then crushed a palace wall, flooding the palace in the process. He launched his Archer Shark attack, injuring Neptune and some of his soldiers. Hody laughed at Neptune for getting in the way of the attack, saying that a king should not protect his subjects. <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a> counterattacked by sending a sword wave at the fish-man. Hody blocked the attack by using one of his own comrades as a shield.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Zoro_Defeats_Hody.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708141959" class="image"><img alt="Zoro Defeats Hody" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Zoro Defeats Hody.png" data-image-key="Zoro_Defeats_Hody.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Zoro_Defeats_Hody.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708141959" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Zoro_Defeats_Hody.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708141959" class="image"><img alt="Zoro Defeats Hody" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Zoro_Defeats_Hody.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708141959" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="130" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Zoro Defeats Hody.png" data-image-key="Zoro_Defeats_Hody.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d4/Zoro_Defeats_Hody.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708141959" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Zoro_Defeats_Hody.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody slashed by Zoro.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hody then ordered his crew to attack, but <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a> held them back by launching a <a href="/wiki/Pop_Green" title="Pop Green">Pop Green</a> that spawns a flower the gives off a bad odor. Hody, however, remained unfazed, commenting on the childishness of the attack. Usopp and <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> untied the guards and Zoro cut Neptune's chains. When completely underwater, Hody prepared to face off against Zoro. However, even though he had an advantage being underwater, he appeared to be no match for the swordsman, who seemed to have dealt him a grievous deep wound.
</p><p>Neptune took Zoro, Usopp, and Brook and created an escape route, which the ministers and the palace guards used to escape. A New Fish-Man Pirate gave Hody an Energy Steroid, reviving him in the process. Before Neptune and the three Straw Hats with him could escape with Hoe, Hody seized Neptune with one hand. The New Fish-Man Pirates then captured Neptune, Zoro, Usopp, and Brook.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Hody_on_TV.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708142044" class="image"><img alt="Hody on TV" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hody on TV.png" data-image-key="Hody_on_TV.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Hody_on_TV.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142044" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Hody_on_TV.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708142044" class="image"><img alt="Hody on TV" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Hody_on_TV.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142044" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hody on TV.png" data-image-key="Hody_on_TV.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/36/Hody_on_TV.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142044" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hody_on_TV.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody making his broadcast.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Hody was later seen addressing Fish-Man Island through a visual broadcast.<sup id="cite_ref-new_scar_11-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-new_scar-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> He explained his plan to take over and rebuild the Ryugu Kingdom with himself as the ruler. He told the citizens that those who wish peace with the humans should be banished. He showed the chained-up King Neptune and explained his plan to execute him in Gyoncorde Plaza in three hours. He went on saying that he found the letter from the World Noble and the box holding the signatures. Since stepping on Otohime's fumi-e would not be enough, he decided to use the signatures to determine who is against him. He would also dispose of anyone who gave their signatures. He then addressed the Straw Hats and showed the imprisoned Zoro, Usopp, and Brook. Hody planned to drown them in a room with rising water after executing Neptune and intended on making an example out of Luffy to the surface world.
</p><p>After he finished his speech, he decided to leave the palace with most of his subordinates since the palace is impenetrable. He was also confident that no one could save the three Straw Hats imprisoned in the palace and commented that the wound he got from Zoro still ached. He then received a status report on the island's new residents from the Fish-Man District. Hody told his subordinates to use the homes of those who left and those who would die.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a2/Energy_Steroid_Side_Effects.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708142206" class="image"><img alt="Energy Steroid Side Effects" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="119" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Energy Steroid Side Effects.png" data-image-key="Energy_Steroid_Side_Effects.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a2/Energy_Steroid_Side_Effects.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142206" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a2/Energy_Steroid_Side_Effects.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708142206" class="image"><img alt="Energy Steroid Side Effects" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a2/Energy_Steroid_Side_Effects.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142206" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="119" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Energy Steroid Side Effects.png" data-image-key="Energy_Steroid_Side_Effects.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a2/Energy_Steroid_Side_Effects.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142206" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Energy_Steroid_Side_Effects.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody succumbing to the Energy Steroid's side effects.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As he was taking the king to Gyoncorde Plaza, he suddenly suffered from intense pain due to taking so many Energy Steroids as painkillers, collapsing and twitching in agony, to the point of having difficulty in breathing. Neptune chastised him for being too reliant on the drug and was now reaping the consequences. Shortly after thrashing around on the sea monster's back that he was riding on, Hody managed to get up, with an apparent change in his body that was enough to frighten a Sea Bear that was a certain distance away.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Battle_for_Fish-Man_Island">Battle for Fish-Man Island</span></h4>
<p>Hody arrived at the execution ground as a changed being. After taking his seat, he then stared quizzically at an Energy Steroid. His crew also gathered at the plaza and the Neptune Army's attempts to save the king were thwarted by the Sea Beasts. When a soldier tried to kill one of the officers with dynamite, Hody stopped him with Uchimizu. With his newfound strength, not only was the shot able to go through the soldier, but it also crashed through several rock and coral formations before landing in the water at Mermaid Cove. He then marveled at his own strength saying that he felt incredible. When the princes arrived, Hody listened to Fukaboshi's speech about how the people want to walk with humans and Hody was preventing that. After the princes defeated the <a href="/wiki/Sea_Beast" title="Sea Beast">Sea Beasts</a>, Hody simply replied that in the end, the kingdom would belong to the victor.
</p><p>The princes were then defeated and captured. Jinbe, Shirahoshi, and Megalo had fallen into one of Hody's traps and got captured as well. Hody was overjoyed that his plan was going smoothly, and all of his subordinates gathered in the plaza. Madam <a href="/wiki/Shyarly" title="Shyarly">Shyarly</a> appeared and told Hody that he would not be the one to destroy Fish-Man Island and the island would be destroyed by Straw Hat Luffy. Out of annoyance, Hody hit her with a water shot and loudly declared on how different he is from her older brother, Arlong. He then revealed to everyone that he was the one who truly assassinated Otohime, stunning the king, the princes, the citizens, Jinbe, and even his lower-rank subordinates. After Hody explained that the human pirate he caught was a scapegoat, Neptune was furious, and Hody responded by injuring him with a water shot. When Hody gloated about killing Otohime right in Shirahoshi's face, the princess said that she knew all along.
</p><p>Surprised, Hody then demanded Shirahoshi to explain how she knew. Shirahoshi explained that Megalo saw Hody committed the crime and told her about it. The reason that Shirahoshi did not tell anyone was because she was honoring her mother's last wish of not holding any hatred towards the killer. Hody then laughed, much to Jinbe's anger, and mocked Megalo for only telling the story to Shirahoshi, saying that if he had told anyone else, his plan would have been ruined. He then ridiculed Shirahoshi, calling her kindness stupidity. He further stated that by hiding the truth, she would lead to the deaths of her father and brothers. When Jinbe tried to reassure Shirahoshi that she did nothing wrong, Hody then tried to prove his point by torturing Neptune and the princes with his water attacks. The citizens could not stand to watch Hody's cruelty any longer and started calling out for Luffy to destroy the island based on Shyarly's prophecy. Hody remained in denial, stating his belief that Shyarly's prediction was a lie. Angry with the citizens, Hody prepared to decapitate Neptune, but Luffy (who had been hiding inside Megalo) appeared and kicked Hody back a great distance.
</p><p>After Hody got back up, he stated on how much he hated fish-men like Jinbe that side with humans. He then revealed his plan to go to the Levely and kill all the kings there. He also stated his goal on becoming Pirate King. Hody ordered his subordinates to attack the Straw Hats, but Luffy easily defeated half of them with <a href="/wiki/Haki" title="Haki">Haki</a>. As Hody was stunned, Luffy told him that he was going to fight him.
</p><p>Hody declared that the Straw Hats could not protect one huge mermaid and proceeded to attack Shirahoshi with a water shot, but his attack was nullified by Jinbe's water shot. Jinbe stated that Hody's level of Fish-Man Karate pales in comparison to Jinbe's. As the Straw Hats took on and begin defeating divisions of the New Fish-Man Pirates one by one, Hody became irritated. He commanded the Kraken to attack, but the Kraken betrayed him for Luffy which angered Hody even more. As the battle continued, Hody threatened to Surume that he would go to the North Pole and kill his brothers if he continued to disobey him. Luffy however overheard this and promised Surume he would protect his brothers before walking toward Hody. Despite Hody's crew trying to stop Luffy, he managed to slip past them and landed a kick on Hody's face.
</p><p>Hody quickly got back up and punched Luffy in the face. The attack had no effect on Luffy since he's rubber. Luffy counterattacked using a headbutt which hit a member of the iron shell division. Luffy then hit Hody again in the stomach, which sent Hody crashing into a wall.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noah_and_Ultimate_Defeat">Noah and Ultimate Defeat</span></h4>
<p>Hody saw that Noah arrived and he cursed Vander Decken IX for trying to destroy Fish-Man Island with him in it. He then climbed up on the chains connecting to Noah while saying this was a good situation. With <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a>'s assistance, Luffy managed to reach on one of the chains attaching to the ship while Hody was somewhere below Luffy. Meanwhile, some of the citizens tried to slow down the boat by pulling on the chains. Hody remarked that their efforts were useless and attacked them with water bullets. The ship continued to rise up after Shirahoshi while Luffy and Hody reached the sea. Hody swam behind Luffy and threatened to kill him, but Luffy was saved by <a href="/wiki/Fukaboshi" title="Fukaboshi">Fukaboshi</a>. Hody then took out a new weapon, Kirisame, and attacked both Luffy and Fukaboshi, but he missed and arrived on Noah.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Hody_Stabs_Decken.png/revision/latest?cb=20230118221353" class="image"><img alt="Hody Stabs Decken" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hody Stabs Decken.png" data-image-key="Hody_Stabs_Decken.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Hody_Stabs_Decken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230118221353" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Hody_Stabs_Decken.png/revision/latest?cb=20230118221353" class="image"><img alt="Hody Stabs Decken" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Hody_Stabs_Decken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230118221353" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="118" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hody Stabs Decken.png" data-image-key="Hody_Stabs_Decken.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/44/Hody_Stabs_Decken.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230118221353" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hody_Stabs_Decken.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody stabs Decken with his trident.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>Decken welcomed Hody, but Hody pierced his trident into Decken without warning while questioning Decken about what would happen to Noah if Decken dies. However, Decken managed to touch Hody with his left hand. Hody stated that if Decken dies, the effects of his ability will disappear. He went on to say that he would let Noah fall on Fish-Man Island. Decken stepped away from Hody and threw an axe at him. Hody easily dodged it and Decken attacked him with his knives installed in his sandals. Hody dodged and bit Decken in the leg. When the axe was coming back, Hody used Decken as a shield and the axe hit Decken instead. After Decken fell, Hody tried to attack Shirahoshi. He repelled <a href="/wiki/Ryuboshi" title="Ryuboshi">Ryuboshi</a> and <a href="/wiki/Manboshi" title="Manboshi">Manboshi</a> and prepared to kill the Mermaid Princess. Luffy, while riding on Fukaboshi's back, grabbed Hody and swinged him away in the nick of time.
</p><p>Hody was undeterred and was still confident that Fish-Man Island would be destroyed. When Shirahoshi changed her course, Hody attempted to stop her, but was once again grabbed by Luffy. When Decken passed out, the ship no longer followed Shirahoshi and began to fall, making Hody pleased by this turn of events.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Gomu_Gomu_no_Red_Hawk.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708142348" class="image"><img alt="Gomu Gomu no Red Hawk" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="139" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Gomu Gomu no Red Hawk.png" data-image-key="Gomu_Gomu_no_Red_Hawk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Gomu_Gomu_no_Red_Hawk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142348" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Gomu_Gomu_no_Red_Hawk.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708142348" class="image"><img alt="Gomu Gomu no Red Hawk" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Gomu_Gomu_no_Red_Hawk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142348" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="139" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Gomu Gomu no Red Hawk.png" data-image-key="Gomu_Gomu_no_Red_Hawk.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b2/Gomu_Gomu_no_Red_Hawk.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708142348" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Gomu_Gomu_no_Red_Hawk.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody struck by Luffy's <b>Red Hawk</b>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>As Luffy and the princes fought against Hody, he kept interfering with their attempts to stop Noah, causing Manboshi to be severely wounded. Luffy punched Hody into the ship, and Hody sliced a hole in the air bubble in retaliation, preventing Luffy from boarding it. Fukaboshi then charged at Hody, questioning what humans had ever done to Hody. Hody's answer was "Nothing" and that he was just passing judgement on the humans, letting the eldest prince know Hody's "true form", which is that of a person born out of hatred and resentment. Hody then tried to stop Luffy and Shirahoshi again, but Luffy broke his Kirisame and sent Hody flying back, and Hody once again got back up. Annoyed, Hody took out a handful of Energy Steroids and consumed them all at once. He started to scream in agony as he underwent another monstrous transformation. Hody was then seen laughing maniacally as Fukaboshi revealed what he learned to Luffy and Fish-Man Island.
</p><p>As Hody moved in, he remembered his past about how Arlong and many other human-hating fish-men taught him and his friends to hate humans, and how he and his crew plotted to overthrow humanity over the years. As he snapped out of memory lane, he was intercepted by Luffy, who declared the end. Hody, accepting the challenge, was prepared to bite off Luffy's arm, but Luffy hit Hody with Gomu Gomu no Red Hawk.
</p><p>After the attack, Hody was sent flying towards Noah and crashed onto the deck of the ship. Wounded so badly, he started attempting to shovel down more Energy Steroids. As he desperately tried to put them back into his mouth, he saw Luffy coming his way. Hody used a new attack called 'Murasame' via the water leaking out of the spot he crashed into. Luffy dodged Hody's attack and counterattacked using Gomu Goum no Elephant Gun, which finally defeated Hody Jones. With his last conscious thought, Hody told Noah to fall on Fish-Man Island to destroy all the fish-men who lost their pride for siding with humanity.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Imprisonment">Imprisonment</span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Hody_and_Decken_Arrested.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708143843" class="image"><img alt="Hody and Decken Arrested" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="192" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hody and Decken Arrested.png" data-image-key="Hody_and_Decken_Arrested.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Hody_and_Decken_Arrested.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708143843" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Hody_and_Decken_Arrested.png/revision/latest?cb=20230708143843" class="image"><img alt="Hody and Decken Arrested" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Hody_and_Decken_Arrested.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708143843" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="192" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hody and Decken Arrested.png" data-image-key="Hody_and_Decken_Arrested.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/0/00/Hody_and_Decken_Arrested.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20230708143843" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hody_and_Decken_Arrested.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody and Decken defeated are arrested after the New Fish-Man Pirates' defeat.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the Sea Kings stopped Noah from crashing into the island, the princes brought the unconscious Hody and Decken to the plaza and put them in chains, with Fukaboshi declaring that these two would be incarcerated forever.<sup id="cite_ref-c648_37-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c648-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Hody, even though unconscious, still had a frightening appearance to him, as his crew said he looked like a monster. Hody, his officers, and Decken were later locked up in the palace prison.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Later on, it is revealed that while in prison, Hody and his officers had aged into old, frail men. The Energy Steroids that they all had been compulsively taking as a way to boost their strength were actually the contents of the <a href="/wiki/Tamatebako" title="Tamatebako">Tamatebako</a>. They were locked up by the Royal Palace due to their dangerous side effects. When the Minister of the Right pointed out an incident in which the Energy Steroids were stolen, Hody confirmed that he was the thief. Despite being frail, Hody swore revenge on both Luffy and Fish-Man Island while called Fukaboshi a disgrace to their race. He was promptly told by Neptune that he would no longer be any threat to the island and that he was truly pitiful, so much so that Neptune said he would reconsider the pirates' punishment. Fukaboshi stated that he does not hate Hody for murdering Otohime, but told him to remain silent as he did not want the children to hear him.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span></h2>
<p>His family name comes from <i><b>hō</b>jiro-zame</i><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">ホオジロザメ</span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, the Japanese name for great white shark.
</p><p>The name "<i>Hody</i>" has been <a href="/wiki/Name_Variants" title="Name Variants">translated</a> as "<i>Hodi</i>", "<i>Hordy</i>", and "<i>Hordi</i>" before being spelt by Oda as "<i>Hody</i>". The FUNimation subs and dub have gone with the translation "<i>Hordy</i>".
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_and_Manga_Differences">Anime and Manga Differences</span></h2>
<ul><li>During his fight against the <a href="/wiki/Gyro" title="Gyro">Gyro Pirates</a>, Hody smashed through the bottom of the ship. In the manga, he caught one of Gyro's men in his mouth while in the anime, the man was simply bashed away when Hody shot out of the floor.</li>
<li>In the anime, when Hody enters the palace, there is a flashback not shown in the manga. It shows that <a href="/wiki/Dosun" title="Dosun">Dosun</a>, as a child, was getting kidnapped by pirates and Hody and the other future officers of the <a href="/wiki/New_Fish-Man_Pirates" title="New Fish-Man Pirates">New Fish-Man Pirates</a> tried to save him only to get beaten down. The pirates prepared to kidnap them as well, but <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a> came and subdued the pirates, saving Hody and his friends.<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
<ul><li>This also conflicts with a statement Hody later states where he admits to Fukaboshi that they have never had any personal interaction with the cruelty of humans that justify their actions. However, this doesn't seem to be the driving force behind his actions against humans, as Hody appears to haven chosen to persecute humans just for the sake of doing so, even before this event took place, as he was a young child upon embracing his malice, and had started attacking humans on purpose by the time Dosun was kidnapped.</li></ul></li>
<li>Hody's battle with Zoro is expanded in the anime.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>When Hody reveals to all fish-men and merfolk gathered at the Gyoncorde Plaza that he is the one who killed Otohime in the anime, he explains how he did it and it's seen in a flashback but it's more seen than explained. In the manga, it's the opposite with Hody's story more explained than seen. The flashback in the anime is clearer than in the manga.</li></ul>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Energy_Steroid_Speed_in_the_Anime.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120930102139" class="image"><img alt="Energy Steroid Speed in the Anime" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="117" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Energy Steroid Speed in the Anime.gif" data-image-key="Energy_Steroid_Speed_in_the_Anime.gif" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Energy_Steroid_Speed_in_the_Anime.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120930102139" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Energy_Steroid_Speed_in_the_Anime.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120930102139" class="image"><img alt="Energy Steroid Speed in the Anime" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Energy_Steroid_Speed_in_the_Anime.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120930102139" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="117" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Energy Steroid Speed in the Anime.gif" data-image-key="Energy_Steroid_Speed_in_the_Anime.gif" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1b/Energy_Steroid_Speed_in_the_Anime.gif/revision/latest?cb=20120930102139" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Energy_Steroid_Speed_in_the_Anime.gif" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody's speed after overdosing on Energy Steroids.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>His fight with Luffy aboard Noah is expanded in the anime with Hody attacking Luffy several times instead of just using Murasame.
<ul><li>This includes the part where Luffy used several <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques#Pre-Timeskip" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">Jet Pistols</a> against him that he was able to evade and Luffy using yet another <a href="/wiki/Gomu_Gomu_no_Mi/Gear_2_Techniques#Gear_2_Haki_Enhanced_Attacks" title="Gomu Gomu no Mi/Gear 2 Techniques">Red Hawk</a>. The finale of the battle is also changed, where in the manga Luffy hits Hody with with a Armament Haki Gear 3 punch after avoiding his Murasame attack. In the anime, Hody uses Murasame to try and push the attack back. It holds for a bit, but ultimately, Luffy's attack gets through and slams into Hody, defeating him.</li></ul></li></ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Appearances">Other Appearances</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Other_Media">Other Media</span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Hody_Jones_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest?cb=20201219203624" class="image"><img alt="Hody Jones Premier Show" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="238" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hody Jones Premier Show.png" data-image-key="Hody_Jones_Premier_Show.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Hody_Jones_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201219203624" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Hody_Jones_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest?cb=20201219203624" class="image"><img alt="Hody Jones Premier Show" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Hody_Jones_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201219203624" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="238" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hody Jones Premier Show.png" data-image-key="Hody_Jones_Premier_Show.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/50/Hody_Jones_Premier_Show.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20201219203624" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hody_Jones_Premier_Show.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Hody in Premier Show 2016.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2014" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2014</a>, <a href="/wiki/Bildy" title="Bildy">Bildy</a> created a <a href="/wiki/Kone_Kone_no_Mi" title="Kone Kone no Mi">fake version</a> of Hody to fight as one of the <a href="/wiki/DX_Marines" title="DX Marines">DX Marines</a>' generals. In <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Premier_Show#One_Piece_Premier_Show_2016" title="One Piece Premier Show">One Piece Premier Show 2016</a>, <a href="/wiki/Pokke" title="Pokke">Pokke</a> created a <a href="/wiki/Mono_Mono_no_Mi" title="Mono Mono no Mi">clone</a> of Hody under <a href="/wiki/Wilder" title="Wilder">Wilder</a>'s order to attack the Straw Hat Pirates.</li>
<li>Hody appears in <a href="/wiki/Tokyo_One_Piece_Tower#One_Piece_4D" title="Tokyo One Piece Tower">One Piece 4D</a>, and an image of him appears in <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Water_Spectacle" title="One Piece Water Spectacle">One Piece Water Spectacle</a>.</li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span></h2>
<ul><li>His given name may come from "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Davy_Jones%27_Locker" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Davy Jones&#39; Locker">Davy Jones</a>", a nickname for what would be the devil or god of the seas.</li>
<li>It is also possible that his name comes from the 1975 thriller film <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Jaws_(film)" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Jaws (film)">Jaws</a></i>, as the Japanese pronunciation for "Jones" <i>Jōnzu</i> (ジョーンズ) and "jaws" <i>Jōzu</i> (ジョーズ) are near-homophones. This is supported by the fact that the titular shark from Jaws was, like Hody, a great white.</li>
<li>A fan asked Oda if Hody has two penises because sharks have them, and Oda answered that yes, Hody has two penises.<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Hody's favorite food is <a href="/wiki/Sea_Beast" title="Sea Beast">Sea Beast</a> meat.<sup id="cite_ref-vivre_card_5-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-vivre_card-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li></ul>

<span style="font-size:x-small"><div class="mw-references-wrap mw-references-columns"><ol class="references">
